<name>J.P. Gonzales<//name><Pics>None< /Pics><response>None<//response><Review>Brian, Maria, and the folks at Merced AAMCO are truly an amazing team! I'm a transfer student who moved to Merced for school. I was about half way through my first semester here with no personal mechanic and a very constrained budget. I first noticed a transmission problem about a month and a half ago: When I'd start driving, my transmission would jerk/kick back as I changed gears, it turns out the transmission range sensor on my 2000 Ford Focus was malfunctioning.

Not sure where to turn, I tried calling my mechanic back home to get some advice, unfortunately he was too busy the times that I called so I had to resort to reviews and word of mouth. I decided to give Merced AAMCO a shot. I was not disappointed!

The whole repair process took about a month for me, mostly due to the restrictiveness of my schedule (I was taking several classes and it was hard for me to get away from school for a day to drop my car off). After purchasing a part online in an attempt to save money, Brian graciously installed the part (I had not asked originally if they accepted customer parts). After about a day, my car started having similar problems, so I brought it back in for another look. Brian and Maria were extremely accommodating: they went out of their way to check the quality of their work, provided me with a fantastic deal that I was not expecting, and EVEN offered to give me a ride to school if I couldn't coordinate a bus route. These guys REALLY cared about my situation as a student and I could not have been more grateful!

It turned out that I had a larger electrical problem in the car, however they were able to take care of the problem and replace the faulty part I had purchased in an afternoon! They even recognized a problem which I had suspected had been going on (excessive vibration and weird idling) which my original mechanic either overlooked or could not recognize. I will be taking my car back in a few days to have them take a look at this problem.

As far as I'm concerned, my experience with the Merced AAMCO crew was nothing but pleasurable and professional. I am very pleased with their service and would recommend them to my new friends here in Merced!

Thanks Merced AAMCO!

< text>
First-
Security, reception and bud tenders - all staff members have been very nice and polite and welcoming! Atmosphere is fun but safe and secure. Never waited longer than 10 mins to enter the shop and that was during their busiest hour.

However, tenders do not seem very knowledgeable about strain origins of the brands they carry, THC levels, quality of high etc.. (If you can tell me "this is an OG strain" i can immediately relate to what the strain has to offer.)
They don't even seem to have a solid grasp of the difference between their pure strains and their hybrids besides the THC levels printed on the box.

It also doesn't help customers that YOU CANT SEE OR SMELL THE FLOWER!
This may be out of the shop's control but regardless - you're spending your hard earned money blindly.
Without a knowledgeable staff to help find the right brand/strain that fits your needs, you might as well close your eyes, spin around and point your finger to choose something.
I got so frustrated the last time i was there, i just ended up getting something that had an interesting name ("cinderella" or something like that) made by Good Flower brand...when i finally got home and opened it up - BLEHH it smelled and tasted awful - chemmy, dry & stale! Literally, i had no further desire to smoke it and ended up giving it away. Am i supposed to bring it back with my receipt for a refund or exchange?
I know the industry is growing and that comes with growing pains but in the meantime, without knowledgeable tenders there to guide you, it makes it difficult to select a quality strain and brand worthy of your money and time - I'm NOT smoking the fancy glass jar or the colorful box or the cute/clever marketing name ("Cinderella" smelled and tasted like one of her ugly step sisters!)
I will not spend more time/money to play guessing games with my weed. Let me see it first, let me smell it first! If not, show me someone who can give me the info i need to make a good choice OR provide customers some kind of recourse if your tender recommends a strain that turns out to be poor quality.
Apologies if this is already offered by the shop, i wasnt aware of any return or exchange options.
Looking forward to seeing this particular business grow and improve their service! Thank you for your efforts and for considering my review/experience.
Best wishes to all!< /text>

< text>
I love B-Dama with all my heart, been a customer of theirs since their restaurant on Piedmont Ave opened. If I could have them cook for me everyday, I'd be in heaven. The set lunches/dinners are some of the best deals around, with a generous portion of fish or other protein, a little salad, a bowl of soup, a nice serving of steamed rice, and another little side of veggies. If you manage to eat the whole thing like me, congratulations on joining the glutton's club!

I'm also a big fan of their tofu salad, with a creamy miso sesame dressing, seaweed, and a brighy hued, spicy oil that brings out a nice contrast to the coolness of the tofu and salad. Their hand rolls are made to order so everything arrives fresh, delicious, and beautiful to boot. Their udon or nabe hits the spot on a chilly day. My husband rotates his meal choice whe we come to Swan's Market, but I'm always in the mood for B-Dama!</text>

< Text>
For me this is the most authentic Japanese food in Oakland. Inside Swan's Market, the B-Dama counter serves up quality dishes at affordable prices: fish collars, nabe pots, sashimi platters, chicken karaage, fish and meats grilled over traditional charcoal hibachis, and an ever-changing menu of daily special menu items, as well as a wide selection of Japanese sakes and a couple beer and wine choices. They also have several very nice bento lunch sets. If you want a more upscale setting and an intimate and amazing 7- or 8-course omakase-style meal, check out their Delage around the corner from B-Dama.<//Text>

5<//Rate>
<text>Recommended! Yummy Japanese food!!

== Food ==
Spicy Tuna roll (4/5)
Yummy! Not quite sure what are the ingredients that went into it other then the rice and spicy roll, but whatever it is, it was really good. One order gets you six pieces.

Tonkotsu (5/5)
Woo, this was super good. The external texture was not too thick and yet still has the crunch and crispness. The meat on the inside was moist and tasty, the accompanying sauce made it even more awesome.

Pork Belly (5/5)
This was an order error but a wonderful mistake. We ordered Salmon belly nigiri but somehow the server heard it as Pork Belly. We saw the chef cooking this through the glass and were drooling at it, in a way delighted that it turned out to be ours.

Cooked over charcoal, the flavour was so awesome. The smell and every bite was just so so good. It came with lettuce to wrap it in which was delicious!

== Ambience ==
This Japanese restaurant sits in a hipster marketplace that has a variety of options such as Mexican, seafood, chicken, pizza etc.

I sat by the bar table with a glass panel to watch the chef/cook in action. The hygiene and cleanliness of the restaurant does make me a less squirm-ish...... compensated by the delicious food.

I will be back! Excited to try the yummy looking udon noodles!< /text>< pics>

Had a great experience this USPS branch when I dropped off my package earlier today. I was trying to get info on the shipping cost for my package, and which shipping option would be most suitable. The person helping me was patient even though I had a lot of questions. He even offered a tape for me to seal my packages. After that, everything was taken care smoothly.

I also saw a customer that only spoke Spanish, but none of the staff speaks Spanish. Rather than getting annoyed, the staff kindly asked the customer to use translation app, and helped them patiently.

Like others, I always had the impression that USPS employees aren't helpful, and in general going to the post office isn't a great experience. That was nothing like the experience I had today. I know it might seem simple, but it definitely matters.< /review>

<userid>104987138528878264636<//userid><Name>Vivek Tiwari<//Name>< date>

< Text>
Writing this review live - I came here for the passport of my new born at 8.30 AM and got a token. Then was asked to stand in a line which had almost 20, 25 folks. They wouldn't start processing the line until 9 AM.  It has been 2.5 hours and I am still standing in the line with my 1 month old baby. I think it will take another 40 minutes before they see me.  What I fail to understand is, why instead of asking you to stand in line, can't they simply call folks by token numbers just like they do in a DMV office? Since it's just 1 booth with 1 processor, calling by token number could be done without any sophisticated equipment - simply put a tablet with token number on top of the window and increment it every-time you are done with an application. There is an ample of free space which they can fill with 10-15 chairs to serve as waiting area.  The whole set-up could be done in less than $300.

I found the current set up as quite horrible and rather insensitive towards customers. These days you don't get this sorta experience even in developing countries!  At the very least, be a little compassionate towards parents with newborns!

EDIT: My number finally came in at 11.30 AM.  The passport submission process in itself was very smooth.  The lady processing it was quite courteous and apologetic for long line and the wait time.< /Text>

This is emargency place to go buy t-shirts.

Pro club t-shirts are sell by size their more than $10.00 each I can go to the Paramount outdoor swap meet  and buy 3 white 2xl pro club t-shirts for the same price.

Shaka t-shirts they sell only on black and white the price are the same by size I can buy 4 2xl Shaka t-shirts at the Montclair outdoor drive through swap meet for half of the price when I buy 4 in there.

Now don't get me wrong like anything else it's it's downs but it has its ups.
Meaning not everything is bad.

If u want Locs glasses they have all Cain's of frames and different styles at way better price from any liquor store, swap meet or mall. A lot of earrings of any Cain for a fair price.<//Review>

<Text>The food here is not all that great but it is not bad. Plus in most cases, I am not a fan of, to begin with. But once in a while, I feel like having something different. This is when I go to Arbys. Having a place in a smaller town like this is excellent. It is because it is something different than most of all those other fast food places.

The staff here is , and the place looks immaculate.
This is always a plus!

The lines are usually not to bad either.

All in all, this is a great place to go if you want something different from the familiar, usually fast food places that you might go to.

I do enjoy the Gyros. Many times you can get them two for six dollars that is a good deal.

Moreover, oh, They have lovely delicious french fries!
They are the best!

They also have rootbeer floats if you are into that kind of stuff. Personally I am not, but I know many are. Most places do not have that as an option. Also, Don't forget their mozzarella cheese sticks those are exceedingly delicious as well.< /Text></record>
